			}

# For RCT - Hippogriffs come to meet the OHS
country_event = {
	id = hippogriff.2
	title = hippogriff.2.t
	desc = hippogriff.2.desc
	
	picture = GFX_event_river_swirl
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Help them
		name = hippogriff.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = hippogriff.3
				hours = 4
				random_hours = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Not Intrested
		name = hippogriff.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = hippogriff.4
				hours = 4
				random_hours = 2
			}
		}
	}
}
# For HIP - OHS says yes
country_event = {
	id = hippogriff.3
	title = hippogriff.3.t
	desc = hippogriff.3.desc
	
	picture = GFX_event_river_swirl
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Great
		name = hippogriff.3.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "La Resistance"
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_ohs_assistance_lar
			add_to_variable = {
				HIP_AHAC_own_operative_detection_chance_factor = -0.25
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				HIP_AHAC_intelligence_agency_defense = 0.75
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_ohs_assistance
			add_to_variable = {
				HIP_AHAC_subversive_activites_upkeep = -0.25
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				HIP_AHAC_foreign_subversive_activites = -0.15
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Anti-harmonic terrorism act
	id = hippogriff.22
	title = hippogriff.22.t
	desc = hippogriff.22.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_minitrue
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Okay
		name = hippogriff.22.a
		set_country_flag = HIP_anti_harmonic_terrorism_act_flag
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_FASCISM
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_NEUTRAL
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = NEUTRAL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = FASCISM
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.025
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			HIP_AHAC_conscription_factor = 0.05
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			HIP_AHAC_war_support_factor = 0.05
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			HIP_AHAC_resistance_garrison_penetration_chance = -0.05
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			HIP_ahac_fascism_drift = 0.02
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_anti_harmonic_terrorism
	}
	option = { #Do Not Sign
		name = hippogriff.22.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_HARMONIST_ALTERNATE
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = HARMONIST_ALTERNATE
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		HIP_violet_facade = {
			add_trait = {
				slot = political_advisor
				trait = HIP_ahac_chief_antifascist
			}
			remove_trait = {
				slot = political_advisor
				trait = HIP_ahac_chief
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HIP_antifascist_violet
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = hippogriff.112
	title = hippogriff.112.t
	desc = {
		text = hippogriff.112.d1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				HIP = {
					has_government = neutrality
					has_government = communism
				}
			}

		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hippogriff.112.d2
		trigger = {
			HIP = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hippogriff.112.d3
		trigger = {
			HIP = {
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_event_aris_and_beach
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff.112"
		hidden_effect = {
			save_event_target_as = alliance_inviter
			FROM = {
				save_event_target_as = alliance_applicant
			}
		}
		}

	option = {#yes
		name = hippogriff.112.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_to_faction = FROM
		FROM = { country_event = { id = generic.3 hours = 6 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = alliance_inviter@ROOT
			FROM = { set_country_flag = alliance_applicant@ROOT }
			news_event = { id = news.289 hours = 12 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {tag = EQS}
			custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_wont_fight_for_db_tt
		}
	}

	option = {#lolnope
		name = hippogriff.112.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = generic.4 hours = 6 }
		}
	}
}

				is_faction_leader = yes
			}

				id = hippogriff.12

			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		}

		}
		add_tech_bonus = {

		}
	}

# HIP - Crack Lightning Returns from his World Tour
country_event = {
	id = hippogriff.16
	title = hippogriff.16.t
	desc = hippogriff.16.desc
	
	picture = GFX_event_green_mountain

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Ok!
		name = hippogriff.16.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_FASCISM
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_NEUTRAL
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = NEUTRAL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = FASCISM
					}
				}
			}
		}
		HIP_increase_divided_society = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}
	option = { # Ok!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_HARMONIST_ALTERNATE
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_COMMUNIST
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_HARMONIST_HISTORICAL
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = HARMONIST_HISTORICAL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = HARMONIST_ALTERNATE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = COMMUNIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = hippogriff.16.b
		HIP_decrease_divided_society = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}
}

# HIP - define harmony
country_event = {
	id = hippogriff.18
	title = hippogriff.18.t
	desc = hippogriff.18.desc
	
	picture = GFX_event_hippogriffianight
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # We're real harmonists
		name = hippogriff.18.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			HIP_AHAC_war_support_factor = 0.05
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_HARMONIST_ALTERNATE
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_COMMUNIST
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_HARMONIST_HISTORICAL
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = HARMONIST_HISTORICAL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = HARMONIST_ALTERNATE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = COMMUNIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = HIP_xenophobic_harmony
	}
	option = { # This is crazy
		name = hippogriff.18.b
		remove_ideas = HIP_violet_facade
		add_ideas = HIP_silverstream
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_FASCISM
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_NEUTRAL
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = NEUTRAL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = FASCISM
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = hippogriff.21
	title = hippogriff.21.t
	desc = hippogriff.21.d
	picture = GFX_event_aris_and_beach
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = hippogriff.21.a
		trigger = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						tag = WAR
						HIP = {
							has_country_flag = HIP_awarded_WAR_TBK
						}
					}
				}
			}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
			}
			add_core_of = HIP
		}

country_event = {
	id = hippogriff.100
	title = hippogriff.100.t
	desc = hippogriff.100.desc
	
	picture = GFX_event_HIP_tank_m1
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = hippogriff.32
				days = 17
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Favour the M1
		name = hippogriff.100.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
			}
			set_technology = {
				basic_light_tank_chassis = 1
			}
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "M2 Light"
				type = light_tank_chassis_1
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					main_armament_slot = tank_small_cannon
					turret_type_slot = tank_light_two_man_tank_turret
					suspension_type_slot = tank_bogie_suspension
					armor_type_slot = tank_riveted_armor
					engine_type_slot = tank_gasoline_engine
					special_type_slot_1 = additional_machine_guns
					special_type_slot_2 = additional_machine_guns
					special_type_slot_3 = additional_machine_guns
				}
				upgrades = {
					tank_nsb_engine_upgrade = 3
					tank_nsb_armor_upgrade = 2
				}
				icon = "gfx/interface/technologies/USA_basic_light_tank.dds"
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_technology = {
				basic_light_tank = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Favour the M2
		name = hippogriff.100.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
			}
			set_technology = {
				basic_heavy_tank_chassis = 1
			}
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "M1 Heavy"
				type = heavy_tank_chassis_1
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					main_armament_slot = tank_close_support_gun
					turret_type_slot = tank_light_three_man_tank_turret
					suspension_type_slot = tank_bogie_suspension
					armor_type_slot = tank_cast_armor
					engine_type_slot = tank_gasoline_engine
					special_type_slot_1 = secondary_turret_small_cannon
					special_type_slot_2 = secondary_turret_hmg
					special_type_slot_3 = additional_machine_guns
					special_type_slot_4 = additional_machine_guns
				}
				upgrades = {
					tank_nsb_engine_upgrade = 2
					tank_nsb_armor_upgrade = 2
				}
				icon = "gfx/interface/technologies/USA_basic_heavy_tank.dds"
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_technology = {
				basic_heavy_tank = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Lets listen to this Cross Tide
		trigger = {
			has_dlc = "No Step Back"
		}
		name = hippogriff.100.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_political_power = -75
		set_technology = {
			basic_light_tank_chassis = 1
			engine_tech_1 = 1
		}
		create_equipment_variant = {
			name = "Clawbeak Tank"
			type = light_tank_chassis_1
			parent_version = 0
			modules = {
				main_armament_slot = tank_small_cannon
				turret_type_slot = tank_light_one_man_tank_turret
				suspension_type_slot = tank_christie_suspension
				armor_type_slot = tank_riveted_armor
				engine_type_slot = tank_gasoline_engine
			}
			upgrades = {
				tank_nsb_engine_upgrade = 8
				tank_nsb_armor_upgrade = 0
			}
			icon = "gfx/interface/technologies/USA_basic_light_tank.dds"
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = hippogriff.25
	title = hippogriff.25.t
	desc = hippogriff.25.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_HIP_warzone

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Well fuck
		name = hippogriff.25.a
		complete_national_focus = HIP_harmonist_defeat
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		set_country_flag = BAT_HIP_defeated

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = HIP_united_society
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HIP_united_society
				add_idea = HIP_divided_society_4
			}
			set_country_flag = HIP_once_united
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_cored_zumidia
				}
			}
			add_ideas = HIP_crisis_2
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = HIP_crisis_1
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_on_equestrian_continent = yes
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
			set_country_flag = {flag = bypass_on_peaceconference_ended value = 1 days = 1}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = HIP
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_on_equestrian_continent = yes
						has_war_with = PREV
					}
					set_country_flag = {flag = bypass_on_peaceconference_ended value = 1 days = 1}
					white_peace = PREV
				}
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
			    is_in_faction = yes 
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = hippogriff.28
				days = 14
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			country_event = {
				id = hippogriff.251
				days = 7
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {add_stability = 0.10}
		}
	}
}

					}

				}

					}

						exists = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = hippogriff.26
					days = 1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				country_event = {
					id = arisfirst.60
					days = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = hippocommie.68
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {#Release CTH
	id = hippogriff.52
	title = hippogriff.52.t
	desc = {
		text = hippogriff.52.d1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = zeirutid_dead
				CVA = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = hippogriff.52.d2
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = zeirutid_dead
					CVA = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_event_colthage_city
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {#No Coltva release
		name = hippogriff.52.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						controller = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							NOT = {
								original_tag = CVA
								original_tag = CDR
							}
						}
						OR = {
							is_core_of = CTH
							is_core_of = CDR
							is_core_of = CVA
						}
					}
				}
				CTH = {transfer_state = PREV}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					1092 = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								tag = HIP
								is_in_faction_with = HIP
							}
						}
					}
				}
				CTH = {transfer_state = 1092}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Coltva release
		name = hippogriff.52.b
		CTH = {
			release = CVA
			hidden_effect = {
				CVA = {
				transfer_technology = yes
				set_research_slots = 2
				load_oob = CVA_civil_war
				complete_national_focus = CVA_the_revolution_has_begun
				set_capital = {
					state = 1093
					remember_old_capital = no
				}
				set_politics = { 
					ruling_party = democratic 
				}
				remove_ideas = CVA_the_fight_for_independence
				complete_national_focus = CVA_the_end_of_the_junta
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 44
					fascism = 0
					communism = 42
					neutrality = 14
				}
				set_country_flag = CVA_cant_ban_neutrality
				set_country_flag = CVA_finished_the_revolution
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				set_cosmetic_tag = CVA_constitutionalist_puppet
				}
			}
		}
		HIP = {
			puppet = CVA
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = CVA
					autonomy_state = autonomy_supervised_state
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = CVA
					autonomy_state = autonomy_colony
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				1097 = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							tag = HIP
							is_in_faction_with = HIP
						}
					}
				}
			}
			CVA = {transfer_state = 1097}
		}
	}
}

				has_country_flag = HIP_BAT_wargames
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {has_tech = trench_warfare}
					BAT = {has_tech = trench_warfare}
				}
				unlock_decision_tooltip = HIP_learn_GBP
				set_country_flag = HIP_can_learn_GBP
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {has_tech = mobile_warfare}
					BAT = {has_tech = mobile_warfare}
				}
				unlock_decision_tooltip = HIP_learn_MW
				set_country_flag = HIP_can_learn_MW
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {has_tech = superior_firepower}
					BAT = {has_tech = superior_firepower}
				}
				unlock_decision_tooltip = HIP_learn_SFP
				set_country_flag = HIP_can_learn_SFP
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {has_tech = mass_assault}
					BAT = {has_tech = mass_assault}
				}
				unlock_decision_tooltip = HIP_learn_MA
				set_country_flag = HIP_can_learn_MA
			}
			else = {
				add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
					name = HIP_wargames
					category = land_doctrine
					uses = 1
					cost_reduction = 0.5
				}
			}
			BAT = {
				add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
					name = HIP_wargames
					category = land_doctrine
					uses = 1
					cost_reduction = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HIP_CTH_wargames
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {has_tech = trench_warfare}
					CTH = {has_tech = trench_warfare}
				}
				unlock_decision_tooltip = HIP_learn_GBP
				set_country_flag = HIP_can_learn_GBP
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {has_tech = mobile_warfare}
					CTH = {has_tech = mobile_warfare}
				}
				unlock_decision_tooltip = HIP_learn_MW
				set_country_flag = HIP_can_learn_MW
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {has_tech = superior_firepower}
					CTH = {has_tech = superior_firepower}
				}
				unlock_decision_tooltip = HIP_learn_SFP
				set_country_flag = HIP_can_learn_SFP
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {has_tech = mass_assault}
					CTH = {has_tech = mass_assault}
				}
				unlock_decision_tooltip = HIP_learn_MA
				set_country_flag = HIP_can_learn_MA
			}
			else = {
				add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
					name = HIP_wargames
					category = land_doctrine
					uses = 1
					cost_reduction = 0.5
				}
			}
			CTH = {
				add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
					name = HIP_wargames
					category = land_doctrine
					uses = 1
					cost_reduction = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = hippogriff.113.t
	desc = hippogriff.113.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_gallus_in_wingbardy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = { # 
		name = hippogriff.113.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					WNG = {
						NOT = {
							has_character = WNG_giovanni_de_gaspwingi
						}
					}
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = WNG_giovanni_de_gaspwingi
					}
					WNG_giovanni_de_gaspwingi = {
						set_nationality = WNG 
					}
				}
			}
		}
		release_puppet = WNG
		WNG = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				long_name = WNG_democratic_party_long
				name = WNG_democratic_party
			}
			WNG_giovanni_de_gaspwingi = {
				promote_character = harmonic_constitutionalism
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # 
		name = hippogriff.113.b
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					WNG = {
						NOT = {
							has_character = WNG_giovanni_de_gaspwingi
						}
					}
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = WNG_giovanni_de_gaspwingi
					}
					WNG_giovanni_de_gaspwingi = {
						set_nationality = WNG 
					}
				}
			}
		}
		release	= WNG
		WNG = {
			set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = no }
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				long_name = WNG_democratic_party_long
				name = WNG_democratic_party
			}
			WNG_giovanni_de_gaspwingi = {
				promote_character = harmonic_constitutionalism
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

				random_days = 5
			}

				id = hipflavour.4
				days = 40
				random_days = 7
			}
		}
	}

		name = hipflavour.2.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.05
		}

		}

country_event = {
	id = hipflavour.3
	title = hipflavour.3.t
	desc = hipflavour.3.desc
	
	picture = GFX_event_aris_first_rally
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HIP_aris_first_founded
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = HIP_aris_first_party_long
				name = HIP_aris_first_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = HIP_aris_first_party_f_long
				name = HIP_aris_first_party_f
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = HIP_raft_wood
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = populism
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					traits = {
						isolationist_advisor
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = HIP_crack_lightning
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = CRACK_LIGHTNING_DESC
					ideology = fascism_ideology
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					traits = {
						HIP_the_ace_leader
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = HIP_block_political_paths
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = arisfirst.2
					months = 7
					random_days = 15
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Its good to see those standing up for our values
		name = hipflavour.3.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.075
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		HIP_decrease_divided_society = yes
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = HIP_aris_first_party_long
				name = HIP_aris_first_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = HIP_aris_first_party_f_long
				name = HIP_aris_first_party_f
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Raft Wood"
				ideology = populism
				picture = "raft_wood.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				traits = {
					isolationist_advisor
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Crack Lightning"
				desc = CRACK_LIGHTNING_DESC
				ideology = fascism_ideology
				picture = "Crack_Lightning.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				traits = {
					HIP_the_ace_leader
				}
			}
		}
		HIP_razorbeak = {
			add_unit_leader_trait = fascist_sympathizer
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 8
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_HARMONIST_ALTERNATE
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_COMMUNIST
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_HARMONIST_HISTORICAL
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = HARMONIST_HISTORICAL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = HARMONIST_ALTERNATE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = COMMUNIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # We must accept progress and not seek to hold on to the past for the sake of it.
		name = hipflavour.3.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.075
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		HIP_increase_divided_society = yes
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = HIP_aris_first_party_long
				name = HIP_aris_first_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = HIP_aris_first_party_f_long
				name = HIP_aris_first_party_f
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Raft Wood"
				ideology = populism
				picture = "raft_wood.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				traits = {
					isolationist_advisor
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Crack Lightning"
				desc = CRACK_LIGHTNING_DESC
				ideology = fascism_ideology
				picture = "Crack_Lightning.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				traits = {
					HIP_the_ace_leader
				}
			}
		}
		HIP_razorbeak = {
			add_unit_leader_trait = fascist_sympathizer
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_NEUTRAL
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_FASCISM
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = NEUTRAL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = FASCISM
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				HIP_is_going_hippogriff = yes
			}
			HIP_decrease_divided_society = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				HIP_is_going_seapony = yes
			}
			HIP_increase_divided_society = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = hipflavour.5.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HIP_siren_takeover
		}
	}

# HIP - Divided Society Sender
country_event = {
	id = hippogriff_society.0
	title = hippogriff_society.0.t
	desc = hippogriff_society.0.desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		country_event = {
			id = hippogriff_society.0
			days = 120
			random_days = 3
		}
	}

	option = { # 
		name = hippogriff_society.0.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HIP_razorbeak_hates_seaponies
			}

		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					HIP_is_going_seapony = yes
				}
				random_list = {
					10 = {
						country_event = {
							id = hippogriff_society.1
							days = 7
							random_days = 6
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					HIP_is_going_hippogriff = yes
				}
				random_list = {
					10 = {
						country_event = {
							id = hippogriff_society.2
							days = 7
							random_days = 6
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = HIP_divided_society_5
				}
				random_list = {
					10 = {
						country_event = {
							id = hippogriff_society.3
							days = 7
							random_days = 6
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				factor = 0.1

			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

	title = arisfirst.4.t
	desc = arisfirst.4.desc

		name = arisfirst.4.a
		set_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = party_popularity@neutrality }
		add_to_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = party_popularity@fascism }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = -0.25 }
			add_stability = stabilitypen_temp
		}
		else = {
			multiply_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = -0.15 }

# Fire at a Car Dealership
country_event = {
	id = arisfirst.5
	title = arisfirst.5.t
	desc = arisfirst.5.desc
	
	picture = GFX_event_rich_set_car
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_war = no
		OR = {
			WNG = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			EQC = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Harmony
		name = arisfirst.5.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = democratic
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {factor = 0}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		set_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = party_popularity@neutrality }
		add_to_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = party_popularity@fascism }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = -0.20 }
			add_stability = stabilitypen_temp
		}
		else = {
			multiply_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = -0.10 }
			add_stability = stabilitypen_temp
		}
	}
	option = { # neither
		name = arisfirst.5.b
		set_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = party_popularity@neutrality }
		add_to_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = party_popularity@fascism }
		ai_chance = {factor = 1}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = -0.10 }
			add_stability = stabilitypen_temp
		}
		else = {
			multiply_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = -0.05 }
			add_stability = stabilitypen_temp
		}
	}
	option = { # non-alligned
		name = arisfirst.5.c
		ai_chance = {factor = 1}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.03
		}
	}
}

# Car Import Protests
country_event = {
	id = arisfirst.11
	title = arisfirst.11.t
	desc = arisfirst.11.desc
	
	picture = GFX_event_eqc_mustang_car
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # We will not ban car imports
		name = arisfirst.11.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 6
			modifier = {
				NOT = { has_government = democratic }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = party_popularity@neutrality }
		add_to_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = party_popularity@fascism }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = -0.10 }
			add_stability = stabilitypen_temp
		}
		else = {
			multiply_temp_variable = { stabilitypen_temp = -0.05 }
			add_stability = stabilitypen_temp
		}
		hidden_effect = {
				if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = HIP_block_political_paths
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = arisfirst.5
					days = 7
					random_days = 1
					}
				}
			}
	}
	option = { # Fine. We will ban them.
		name = arisfirst.11.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				has_government = democratic
				factor = 0.75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			add_political_power = -75
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = arisfirst_car_ban_tt
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.025
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.025
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					WNG = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = {
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
				}
				WNG = {
					country_event = {
						id = arisfirst.16
						days = 1
						random_hours = 4
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					EQC = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = {
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
				}
				EQC = {
					country_event = {
						id = arisfirst.16
						days = 1
						random_hours = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
# Hippogriffia banned imports of our cars!
country_event = {
	id = arisfirst.16
	title = arisfirst.16.t
	desc = arisfirst.16.desc
	
	picture = GFX_event_rich_set_car
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # We will issue a diplomatic protest
		name = arisfirst.16.a
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = HIP_car_ban_modifier
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = arisfirst.17
				days = 1
				random_hours = 4
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
	option = { # We shall react with equivelent bans
		name = arisfirst.16.b
		add_political_power = 25
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = HIP_car_ban_modifier
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = HIP_car_ban_trade_modifier
			}
			country_event = {
				id = arisfirst.18
				days = 1
				random_hours = 4
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = arisfirst.42
	title = arisfirst.42.t
	desc = arisfirst.42.desc
	
	picture = GFX_event_aris_first_rally
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Welp that happened
		name = arisfirst.42.a
		complete_national_focus = HIP_hippogriffia_first
		effect_tooltip = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Raft Wood and Crack Lightning"
				desc = "ARISFIRST_DUUMVIRATE_DESC"
				picture = "HIP_arisfirst_duumvirate.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = populism
				traits = {
					uneasy_duumvirate
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			HIP_raft_wood = {
				set_character_name = HIP_af_duumvirate
				remove_advisor_role = { slot = political_advisor }
				set_portraits = {
					civilian = {
						large = "gfx/leaders/HIP/HIP_arisfirst_duumvirate.tga"
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = HIP_duumvirate_active
				remove_country_leader_role = { ideology=populism }
				
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes

					country_leader = {
						desc = "ARISFIRST_DUUMVIRATE_DESC"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = populism
						traits = {
							uneasy_duumvirate
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_ideas = HIP_figurehead_novo
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = HIP_screaming_eagle
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = hippogriff_news.2
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = arisfirst.43
				days = 40
				}
			}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HIP_arisfirst_government
		}
	}
}

# Crack has Raft killed
country_event = {
	id = arisfirst.46
	title = arisfirst.46.t
	desc = arisfirst.46.d
	
	picture = GFX_event_gothic_interior
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = arisfirst.46.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.15 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = -0.10 }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = HIP_figurehead_novo
			add_idea = HIP_hostage_novo
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = HIP_sky_beak	
		}
		HIP_violet_facade = {
			retire = yes
		}
		HIP_raft_wood = {

country_event = {#Moonfeather becomes oil baron
	id = arisfirst.57
	title = arisfirst.57.t
	desc = {text = arisfirst.57.d1 trigger = {has_country_flag = HIP_ZAR_interests}} #Figure out how to determine if you have control of ZAR
	desc = {text = arisfirst.57.d2 trigger = {NOT = {has_country_flag = HIP_ZAR_interests}}}
	picture = GFX_event_gothic_interior
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = arisfirst.57.a
		add_ideas = limited_exports
		trigger = {has_country_flag = HIP_ZAR_interests}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = HIP_public_private_partnership
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HIP_public_private_partnership
				add_idea = HIP_monopolised_economy_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = HIP_wood_high_interest_bonds
					has_completed_focus = HIP_arisfirst_war_bonds
				}
			}
			add_ideas = HIP_monopolised_economy_2
		}

			add_ideas = HIP_monopolised_economy_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					755 = {
						has_resources_amount = {
							resource = oil
							amount > 0
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = HIP_funding_oilfields_1
				days = 120
			}
		}
		give_resource_rights = {receiver = HIP state = 878}
		give_resource_rights = {receiver = HIP state = 755}
		give_resource_rights = {receiver = HIP state = 756}
	}
	option = {
		name = arisfirst.57.b
		add_ideas = limited_exports
		trigger = {has_country_flag = HIP_ZAR_interests}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {

						amount > 0
					}
				}
				}
			}

				days = 120
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = HIP_public_private_partnership
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HIP_public_private_partnership
				add_idea = HIP_monopolised_economy_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = HIP_wood_high_interest_bonds
					has_completed_focus = HIP_arisfirst_war_bonds
				}
			}
			add_ideas = HIP_monopolised_economy_2
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = HIP_monopolised_economy_1
		}
		give_resource_rights = {receiver = HIP state = 878}
		give_resource_rights = {receiver = HIP state = 755}
		give_resource_rights = {receiver = HIP state = 756}
	}

			}

country_event = {#puppet or balkanize
	id = arisfirst.72
	title = arisfirst.72.t
	desc = arisfirst.72.d

	picture = GFX_event_colthage_city
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {#puppet
		name = arisfirst.72.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				CTH = {
					exists = no
				}
			}
			release_puppet = CTH
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				CTH = {
					is_subject_of = HIP
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CTH
				}
				transfer_state_to = CTH
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {is_core_of = CDR}
			transfer_state_to = CTH
			add_claim_by = CTH
		}
		every_owned_state = {

country_event = { # The Withdrawal
	id = arisfirst.102
	title = arisfirst.102.t
	desc = arisfirst.102.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_event_zebrica_9

	option = { # time to turn everything into a shithole
		name = arisfirst.102.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				WAR = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			annex_country = { target = WAR }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ZAR = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			annex_country = { target = ZAR }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TBK = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			annex_country = { target = TBK }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				WAR = {exists = no}
			}
			release = WAR
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ZAR = {
					exists = no
				}
			}
			release = ZAR
			set_country_flag = HIP_ZAR_interests
			ZAR = {
				add_stability = -0.5
				add_war_support = -0.5
				add_ideas = tribal_society
				set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality  elections_allowed = no } 
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = ZAR_regency_council
					country_leader = {
						desc = ZAR_regency_desc
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = tribal_council
						traits = { }
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					load_focus_tree = generic_zebra_focus
				}
			}
		}
		
	every_state = { # Checks for Tobuckian States
			limit = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						state = 1205
						state = 692
						state = 728
						state = 745
						state = 729
						}
					is_owned_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
				}
			}
			add_core_of = WAR
			WAR = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				WAR = {
					any_owned_state = {
						is_core_of = TBK
					}
				}
			}
			WAR = {
				add_stability = -0.30
				add_manpower = -12000
			}
		}
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {division_template = "Last Warband"}
		clr_country_flag = HIP_has_last_warband
	}
}

	}

		name = arisfirst.103.b
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					WNG = {
						NOT = {
							has_character = WNG_prince_gumberto
						}
					}
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = WNG_prince_gumberto
					}
					WNG_prince_gumberto = {
						set_nationality = WNG 
					}
				}
			}
		}
		release_puppet = WNG
		WNG = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				name = WNG_monarchy_party
				long_name = WNG_monarchy_party_long
			}
			WNG_prince_gumberto = {
				add_country_leader_trait = prince_of_blackwings
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = nazism
						traits = { prince_of_blackwings }
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Who to have as puppet in WNG?
	id = hippocommie.133
	title = hippocommie.133.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = RWP_H_formed
		}
		text = hippocommie.133.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = RWP_H_formed
			}
		}
		text = hippocommie.133.d2
	}
	picture = GFX_event_HIP_posada_hydrogen_atom
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #Bordiclaw
		name = hippocommie.133.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					WNG = {
						NOT = {
							has_character = WNG_griffmadeo_bordiga
						}
					}
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = WNG_griffmadeo_bordiga
					}
					WNG_griffmadeo_bordiga = {
						set_nationality = WNG 
					}
				}
			}
		}
		release_puppet = WNG
		WNG = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = WNG_posada
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = WNG_griffmadeo_bordiga
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = anti_revisionism
					desc = ""
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					traits = {
						marxist_philosopher
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Proletarino
		name = hippocommie.133.b
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					WNG = {
						NOT = {
							has_character = WNG_antonino_proletarino
						}
					}
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = WNG_antonino_proletarino
					}
					WNG_antonino_proletarino = {
						set_nationality = WNG 
					}
				}
			}
		}
		release_puppet = WNG
		WNG = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = WNG_posada
		}
	}
	option = { #Gacci
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = RWP_H_formed
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					WNG = {
						NOT = {
							has_character = WNG_giovanni_gacci
						}
					}
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = WNG_giovanni_gacci
					}
					WNG_giovanni_gacci = {
						set_nationality = WNG 
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = hippocommie.133.c
		release_puppet = WNG
		WNG = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = WNG_posada
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				long_name = WNG_psw_long
				name = WNG_psw
			}
			WNG_giovanni_gacci = {
				promote_character = democratic_socialism
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Motor Strike
	id = hippogriff_communist.2
	title = hippogriff_communist.2.t
	desc = {
		text = hippogriff_communist.2.d
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HIP_unions_banned
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hippogriff_communist.2.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HIP_unions_banned
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_event_manehattan_protest
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { # hear them out
		name = hippogriff_communist.2.a
		set_country_flag = HIP_commies_happy_2
		add_political_power = -15
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_COMMUNIST
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = COMMUNIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # They should return to work
		name = hippogriff_communist.2.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Popular march
	id = hippogriff_communist.8
	title = hippogriff_communist.8.t
	desc = hippogriff_communist.8.d
	picture = GFX_event_manehattan_protest
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { # Don't shoot!
		name = hippogriff_communist.8.a
		set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = yes }
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = communism
			long_name = HIP_RWP_party_long
			name = HIP_RWP_party
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = HIP_posada
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = marxism
				desc = "HIP_POSADA_DESC"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				traits = {
					nuclear_revolutionary
				}
			}
		}
		add_ideas = HIP_seapony_antipathy
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { 
				target = HIP 
				modifier = CHN_Embargo 
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { 
				target = HIP
				modifier = CHN_Embargo 
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = HIP
				modifier = mortal_enemies
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = HIP
				modifier = mortal_enemies
			}
		}
		HIP_stratus_skyranger = {
			retire = yes
		}
		HIP_lucy_duskfeather = {
			retire = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # A brawl is surely brewing, now go!
	id = hippogriff_abyss.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff_abyss.3"}
	title = hippogriff_abyss.3.t
	desc = hippogriff_abyss.3.d
	#picture = TODO
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { # We'll deal with this ourselves
		name = hippogriff_abyss.3.a
		add_timed_idea = { idea = HIP_maintaining_order days = 120 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = hippogriff_abyss.4
				days = 120
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_ABYSS
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = ABYSS
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # SEND IN THE ELEMENTS
		name = hippogriff_abyss.3.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_elements_option_tt
		EQS = {
			country_event = {
				id = hippogriff_abyss.5
				days = 3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_AI_ABYSS
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HIP_ai_behavior
						option = ABYSS
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Let's just hope this goes away naturally
		name = hippogriff_abyss.3.c
		add_political_power = 200
		set_stability = 0.7
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.5 }
		}
		set_country_flag = HIP_cultists_actions
		set_country_flag = HIP_block_political_paths
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_cultist_path_tt
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = fascism
			name = HIP_cultists_party
			long_name = HIP_cultists_party_long
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = HIP_cultist_leader
			promote_leader = yes

			country_leader = {
				desc = ""
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = nazism
				traits = { }
			}
		}
		remove_country_leader_trait = queen_of_the_hippogriffs
		hidden_effect = {
			EQC = {
				country_event = { id = mareland.8 days = 17 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Hippogriff civil war
	id = hippogriff_abyss.12
	title = hippogriff_abyss.12.t
	desc = hippogriff_abyss.12.d
	#picture = TODO
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff_abyss.12"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { original_tag = ZUM }
					owns_state = 698
					has_full_control_of_state = 698
					owns_state = 697
					has_full_control_of_state = 697
					owns_state = 711
					has_full_control_of_state = 711
					owns_state = 710
					has_full_control_of_state = 710
				}
				release = ZUM
			}
			add_stability = 0.3
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = HIP
					NOT = { has_state_flag = HIP_has_cultist_support }
				}
				set_state_flag = HIP_has_no_cultist_support
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = HIP_has_cultist_support
				}
				HIP = { set_capital = { 
					state = PREV 
					remember_old_capital = no
				} }
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				ideology = democratic
				size = 0.5
				states = all
				states_filter = {
					has_state_flag = HIP_has_no_cultist_support
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.51
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = HIP
					has_government = democratic
				}
				save_event_target_as = HIP_siren_civil_war
				HIP = {
					transfer_navy = { target = PREV }
				}
			}
			event_target:HIP_siren_civil_war = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 1165
					}
					set_capital = { state = 1165 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 1202
					}
					set_capital = { state = 1202 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 685
					}
					set_capital = { state = 685 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 1204
					}
					set_capital = { state = 1204 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 684
					}
					set_capital = { state = 684 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 686
					}
					set_capital = { state = 686 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 1203
					}
					set_capital = { state = 1203 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 683
					}
					set_capital = { state = 683 }
				}
				else = {
					random_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_on_continent = africa
						}
						event_target:HIP_siren_civil_war = { set_capital = { state = PREV } }
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:HIP_siren_civil_war = {
				division_template = {
					name = "Loyalist Brigade"
					priority = 1
					is_locked = yes
					regiments = {
						militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_on_continent = africa
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Loyalist Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0 start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = HIP
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = HIP_loyalist
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = hippogriff_abyss.12.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_siren_civil_war_tt
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = hippogriff_news.5 days = 1 } }
		division_template = {
			name = "Cultist Brigade"
			priority = 1
			is_locked = yes
			regiments = {
				militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_on_continent = africa
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Cultist Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0 start_equipment_factor = 1"
				owner = ROOT
			}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff_abyss.32"}
	title = hippogriff_abyss.32.t
	desc = hippogriff_abyss.32.d
	#picture = TODO
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { # who says we need to put it out lmao, keep it burning
		name = hippogriff_abyss.32.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_colthage_adagio_path_tt
		set_country_flag = HIP_SIR_colthage_adagio
	}
	option = { # break this factionalism and keep this place under control
		name = hippogriff_abyss.32.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_colthage_aria_path_tt
		set_country_flag = HIP_SIR_colthage_aria
	}
}

country_event = { # so who are we gonna give the land to
	id = hippogriff_abyss.33
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff_abyss.33"}
	title = hippogriff_abyss.33.t
	desc = {
		text = hippogriff_abyss.33.d1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				HIE = {
					has_country_flag = HIE_CTH_won_the_civil_war
				}
			}
			has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_colthage_aria
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hippogriff_abyss.33.d2
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				HIE = {
					has_country_flag = HIE_CTH_won_the_civil_war
				}
			}
			has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_colthage_adagio
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hippogriff_abyss.33.d3
		trigger = {
			HIE = {
				has_country_flag = HIE_CTH_won_the_civil_war
			}
		}
	}
	#picture = TODO
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { # to pride and profits of landowners!
		name = hippogriff_abyss.33.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				HIE = {
					has_country_flag = HIE_CTH_won_the_civil_war
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = CTH
					is_core_of = TRO
					is_core_of = HIE
					is_core_of = CVA
					is_core_of = CDR
				}
			}
			add_resistance = -5
			add_compliance = 10
		}
		add_to_variable = { HIP_SIR_colthage_landowners_level = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_landowners_influence_up
	}
	option = { # don't you just love land reform
		name = hippogriff_abyss.33.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				HIE = {
					has_country_flag = HIE_CTH_won_the_civil_war
				}
			}
			has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_colthage_adagio
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = CTH
					is_core_of = TRO
					is_core_of = HIE
					is_core_of = CVA
					is_core_of = CDR
				}
			}
			add_resistance = 15
			add_compliance = 15
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = zeirutid_dead
				}
			}
			country_event = hippogriff_abyss_flavor.14
		}
	}
	option = { # wow the star father really messed this place up (1)
		name = hippogriff_abyss.33.c
		trigger = {
			HIE = {
				has_country_flag = HIE_CTH_won_the_civil_war
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = CTH
					is_core_of = TRO
					is_core_of = HIE
					is_core_of = CVA
					is_core_of = CDR
				}
			}
			add_compliance = 10
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

	}
	desc = {

			has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_colthage_adagio
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

					is_core_of = HIE
					is_core_of = CVA
					is_core_of = CDR
				}
			}
			add_resistance = -10
			add_compliance = 5
		}
		set_temp_variable = { HIP_SIR_magic_change_var = -30 }
		HIP_SIR_magic_change = yes
		add_to_variable = { HIP_SIR_colthage_authority_level = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_authority_influence_up
		add_to_variable = { HIP_SIR_colthage_landowners_level = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_landowners_influence_up
	}
	option = { # colthage is dead, long live colthage
		name = hippogriff_abyss.35.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_colthage_adagio
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = CTH
					is_core_of = TRO
					is_core_of = HIE
					is_core_of = CVA
					is_core_of = CDR
				}
			}
			add_resistance = 5
			add_compliance = 10
		}
		set_temp_variable = { HIP_SIR_magic_change_var = 30 }
		HIP_SIR_magic_change = yes
		subtract_from_variable = { HIP_SIR_colthage_authority_level = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_authority_influence_down
		add_to_variable = { HIP_SIR_colthage_warlords_level = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_warlords_influence_up
	}
}

		custom_effect_tooltip = SOL_Faith_Sacrifice_Worship_tp
		hidden_effect = {

				popup = no

			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_rule = {
				can_use_kamikaze_pilots = yes
			}
			set_country_flag = kamikaze_flag
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = kamikaze_focus_tooltip
	}
	option = { # yeah no thanks lmao
		name = hippogriff_abyss.38.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = FRN_hospital_train_tech_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_technology = {
				popup = no

			}
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = hospital_research

		}
	}

country_event = { # white-peace with Wingbardy for Abyssinia
	id = hippogriff_abyss.42
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff_abyss.42"}
	title = hippogriff_abyss.42.t
	desc = hippogriff_abyss.42.d
	#picture = TODO
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { # coolio
		name = hippogriff_abyss.42.a
		set_country_flag = { flag = bypass_on_peaceconference_ended days = 1 value = 1 }
		white_peace = WNG
		set_truce = { target = WNG days = 365 }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_subject_of = WNG
					is_in_faction_with = WNG
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = { flag = bypass_on_peaceconference_ended days = 1 value = 1 }
			white_peace = HIP
			set_truce = { target = HIP days = 365 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ABY = {
					exists = yes
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = ABY
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = ABY
					is_core_of = MDL
				}
				NOT = {
					owner = {
						tag = HIP
					}
				}
			}
			HIP = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff_abyss.57"}
	title = hippogriff_abyss.57.t
	desc = hippogriff_abyss.57.d
	#picture = TODO
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { # ew commies
		name = hippogriff_abyss.57.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						tag = CHN
						is_subject_of = CHN
					}
				}
				OR = {
					region = 65
					state = 241
					state = 333
					state = 233
					state = 168
					state = 162
					state = 160
					state = 164
					state = 157
					state = 326
					state = 156
					state = 154
					state = 155
					state = 102
				}
			}
			HIP = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_country_flag = HIP_CHN_gave_up_stalliongrad
		HIP = {
			set_country_flag = HIP_SIR_siren_stalliongrad
			set_country_flag = HIP_SIR_stalliongrad_negotiated
			country_event = hippogriff_abyss.64
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				HIP = {
					owns_state = 153
				}
				add = 30
			}
			modifier = {
				HIP = {
					owns_state = 57
				}
				add = 20
			}
			modifier = {
				HIP = {
					owns_state = 225
				}
				add = 15
			}
			modifier = {
				HIP = {
					owns_state = 235
				}
				add = 15
			}
			modifier = {
				HIP = {
					owns_state = 233
				}
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				HIP = {
					owns_state = 332
				}
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				HIP = {
					owns_state = 157
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = HIP_CHN_gave_up_southwest
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = HIP_CHN_gave_up_manehattan
				factor = 0.8
			}
			modifier = {
				HIP = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_changeling_southwest
				}
				factor = 1.25
			}
			modifier = {
				HIP = {
					has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_changeling_canterlot
				}
				factor = 1.3
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # but I'm a Not!Dieter simp
		name = hippogriff_abyss.57.b
		HIP = {
			country_event = hippogriff_abyss.65
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

					state = 114

					state = 66
				}
			}

		}

country_event = { # Negotiations - Status of the Crystal Empire
	id = hippogriff_abyss.60
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff_abyss.60"}
	title = hippogriff_abyss.60.t
	desc = hippogriff_abyss.60.d
	#picture = TODO
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { # it's ours lmao
		name = hippogriff_abyss.60.a
		trigger = {
			HIP = {
				owns_state = 344
				owns_state = 345
				OR = {
					owns_state = 152
					owns_state = 98
				}
				OR = {
					owns_state = 53
					owns_state = 151
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_changeling_stalliongrad
				has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_changeling_canterlot
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						tag = CHN
						is_subject_of = CHN
					}
				}
				OR = {
					region = 70
					region = 71
					state = 147
					state = 55
					state = 64
					state = 339
				}
			}
			HIP = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_country_flag = HIP_SIR_siren_crystal_empire
		set_country_flag = HIP_SIR_crystal_empire_negotiated
		ai_chance = { factor = 200 }
	}
	option = { # we'll have to ask them
		name = hippogriff_abyss.60.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owns_state = 344
				owns_state = 152
				owns_state = 98
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_changeling_stalliongrad
				has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_changeling_canterlot
			}
		}
		CHN = {
			country_event = {
				id = hippogriff_abyss.61
				days = 2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 2 }
	}

				}

country_event = { # Our future relationship with CHN
	id = hippogriff_abyss.66
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff_abyss.66"}
	title = hippogriff_abyss.66.t
	desc = hippogriff_abyss.66.d
	#picture = TODO
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { # expand our relations, we can learn from each other for now
		name = hippogriff_abyss.66.a
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = CHN
			has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_negotiations_successful
		}
		CHN = {
			country_event = hippogriff_abyss.67
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 200 }
	}
	option = { # the current situation suits us fine
		name = hippogriff_abyss.66.b
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = CHN
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.05
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
	}
	option = { # cut off relations, we're done
		name = hippogriff_abyss.66.c
		if = {

		}
	}

	desc = hippogriff_abyss.1009.d
	#picture = TODO

	fire_only_once = no

		name = hippogriff_abyss.1009.a
		add_ideas = HIP_SIR_magic_deficit
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_how_to_unfuck_yourself_tt
	}
}

country_event = { # Uh oh, everyone's angry
	id = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff_abyss_resistance.1"}
	title = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.1.t
	desc = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.1.d
	#picture = TODO
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { # oh god oh fu-
		name = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.1.a
		set_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_stability_factor = -0.2 }
		set_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_war_support_factor = -0.2 }
		set_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_political_power_gain = -0.5 }
		set_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_industrial_capacity_factory = -0.2 }
		set_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_industrial_capacity_dockyard = -0.2 }
		set_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_magic_drift = -3.00 }
		
		hidden_effect = {
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = HIP_SIR_united_aris_resistance
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				EQS = {
					exists = yes
					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
			EQS = {
				country_event = { id = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.3 days = 6 }
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
		    ideology = democratic
			name = HIP_SIR_resistance_party
			long_name = HIP_SIR_resistance_party_long
		}
		set_party_name = {
		    ideology = neutrality
			name = HIP_SIR_resistance_party
			long_name = HIP_SIR_resistance_party_long
		}
		set_party_name = {
		    ideology = communism
			name = HIP_SIR_resistance_party
			long_name = HIP_SIR_resistance_party_long
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = HIP_posada
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = "HIP_POSADA_DESC"
				ideology = marxism
				expire="1965.1.1"
				traits = {
					nuclear_revolutionary
				}
			}

		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = HIP_skystar
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				desc = "HIP_SKYSTAR_DESC"
				ideology = conservatism
				expire="1965.1.1"
				traits = {
					eccentric_royal
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HIP_SIR_resistance_formed
			set_variable = { HIP_SIR_resistance_unity_level = 3 }
			set_variable = { HIP_SIR_resistance_skystar_level = 4 }
			set_variable = { HIP_SIR_resistance_lightning_level = 3 }
			set_variable = { HIP_SIR_resistance_posada_level = 2 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # THE MANE SIX ARE HERE OH GOD OH FU-
	id = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.4
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff_abyss_resistance.4"}
	title = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.4.t
	desc = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.4.d
	#picture = TODO
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { # NO NO NO OH GOD
		name = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.4.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = HIP_SIR_break_them_apart
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_magic_drift = 1.00 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_RES_elements_2
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_magic_drift = 2.00 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_RES_elements_1
		}
		set_country_flag = HIP_SIR_elements_present
		set_country_flag = HIP_SIR_resistance_elements_flag
	}
}

country_event = { # The resistance is gone :crabrave:
	id = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.8
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff_abyss_resistance.8"}
	title = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.8.t
	desc = {
		text = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.8.d1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_elements_present
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.8.d2
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_elements_present
			}
		}
	}
	#picture = TODO
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { # WOOOOOOOOO
		name = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.8.a
		add_to_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_industrial_capacity_factory = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_industrial_capacity_dockyard = 0.05 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_resistance_collapse1_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { HIP_SIR_resistance_lightning_level = 2 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_stability_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_war_support_factor = 0.05 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_resistance_collapse2_tt
			set_country_flag = HIP_SIR_crack_lightning_weakened
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HIP_SIR_elements_present
			}
			add_to_variable = { HIP_RESISTANCE_magic_drift = 1.00 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_resistance_collapse3_tt
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_resistance_faction_actions_tt
	}
}

country_event = { #You've been hit by, you've been struck by, MUSICAL EQUIPMENT *M6 Edition*
	id = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.15
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hippogriff_abyss_resistance.15"}
	title = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.15.t
	desc = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.15.d
	#picture = TODO
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { #phat oof bro
		name = hippogriff_abyss_resistance.15.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = HIP_SIR_unfinished_content_tt
		clr_country_flag = HIP_siren_takeover
		clr_country_flag = trade_laws_blocked
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			add_stability = 0.4
			set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = no }
			remove_ideas = HIP_SIR_adagio_advisor
			remove_ideas = HIP_SIR_aria_advisor
			remove_ideas = HIP_SIR_sonata_advisor
			remove_ideas = HIP_SIR_plumage_moonfeather
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = HIP_SIR_divided_society
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = HIP_SIR_divided_society
					add_idea = HIP_divided_society_5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = HIP_siren_economy
				}
				add_ideas = low_economic_mobilisation
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = HIP_siren_conscription
				}
				add_ideas = limited_conscription
			}
			add_ideas = HIP_royal_line_of_novo
			EQS = {
				clr_country_flag = EQS_HIP_elements_sent
			}
			load_focus_tree = HIP_dummy_tree
		}
	}
}

							character = CVA_zeshmunazash_zeirutid

						}
					}
				}

							original_tag = TBK

								character = TBK_alesia

							}
						}

							has_government = fascism
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = hippogriff_news.7.e
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							original_tag = BAT
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = BAT_national_catastrophe
							}
						}
						original_tag = HIE

				}
				OR = {

					}
					HIP = {

		}
	}
